# Variables by Topic or Module

This page provides a topical index of GSS variables based on the modules
and subject areas that each variable is connected to, based on the GSSâ€™s
own classification. Survey modules are groups of questions that were
designed to be fielded together, and are closely related for that
reason. Subject classifications are for convenience and are not meant to
be exclusive or exhaustive.
